                        "\"\"\"\nB2B SaaS MVP: Automated Dispute Evidence Collection & Submission\n\nFeatures:\n- Evidence collection from Shopify (orders, customer info)\n- Redacted & watermarked PDF generation using Puppeteer (via pyppeteer)\n- Integration with Stripe & PayPal APIs for dispute submission\n- Secure PII handling (encryption at rest)\n- Job queue for async processing (using RQ & Redis)\n- Simple Flask API for job submission and status tracking\n\nRequirements:\n- pip install flask pyppeteer stripe paypalrestsdk rq redis cryptography python-dotenv shopifyapi\n\nNote: Set up Redis server and .env file with API keys before running.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport io\nimport json\nimport uuid\nimport tempfile\nfrom flask import Flask, request, jsonify, send_file\nfrom redis import Redis\nfrom rq import Queue\nfrom cryptography.fernet import Fernet\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\nimport stripe\nimport paypalrestsdk\nimport shopify\nfrom pyppeteer import launch\nimport asyncio\n\n# Load environment variables\nload_dotenv()\n\n# --- Configurations ---\nSTRIPE_API_KEY = os.getenv('STRIPE_API_KEY')\nPAYPAL_CLIENT_ID = os.getenv('PAYPAL_CLIENT_ID')\nPAYPAL_CLIENT_SECRET = os.getenv('PAYPAL_CLIENT_SECRET')\nSHOPIFY_API_KEY = os.getenv('SHOPIFY_API_KEY')\nSHOPIFY_PASSWORD = os.getenv('SHOPIFY_PASSWORD')\nSHOPIFY_SHOP_NAME = os.getenv('SHOPIFY_SHOP_NAME')\nFERNET_KEY = os.getenv('FERNET_KEY') or Fernet.generate_key().decode()\nREDIS_URL = os.getenv('REDIS_URL', 'redis://localhost:6379')\n\n# --- Initialize Services ---\nstripe.api_key = STRIPE_API_KEY\npaypalrestsdk.configure({\n    \"mode\": \"live\",  # Step 2: Prepare HTML evidence\n    html = f\"<h1>Order Evidence</h1><pre>{json.dumps(order_data, indent=2)}</pre>\"\n    html = redact_html(html, [pii_data[k] for k in pii_fields if pii_data[k]])\n    html = watermark_html(html, watermark_text)\n\n    # Step 3: Generate PDF (async)\n    pdf_bytes = asyncio.run(html_to_pdf(html))\n\n    # Step 4: Submit to gateway\n    if gateway == 'stripe':\n        file_id = submit_stripe_dispute(pdf_bytes, dispute_id)\n        result = {'status': 'submitted', 'file_id': file_id}\n    elif gateway == 'paypal':\n        response = submit_paypal_dispute(pdf_bytes, dispute_id)\n        result = {'status': 'submitted', 'response': response}\n    else:\n        result = {'status': 'failed', 'error': 'Unknown gateway'}\n\n    # Step 5: Store encrypted PII for audit (simulate DB)\n    audit_id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n    redis_conn.set(f\"pii:{audit_id}\", encrypted_pii)\n\n    return {'result': result, 'audit_id': audit_id}\n\n# --- API Endpoints ---\n\n@app.route('/submit_dispute', methods=['POST'])\ndef submit_dispute():\n    \"\"\"\n    Request JSON:\n    {\n        \"order_id\": \"...\",\n        \"gateway\": \"stripe\" | \"paypal\",\n        \"dispute_id\": \"...\",\n        \"watermark\": \"Confidential\"\n    }\n    \"\"\"\n    data = request.json\n    job = queue.enqueue(\n        process_dispute_job,\n        data['order_id'],\n        data['gateway'],\n        data['dispute_id'],\n        data.get('watermark', 'Confidential')\n    )\n    return jsonify({'job_id': job.id})\n\n@app.route('/job_status/<job_id>', methods=['GET'])\ndef job_status(job_id):\n    \"\"\"Check job status/result.\"\"\"\n    job = queue.fetch_job(job_id)\n    if not job:\n        return jsonify({'status': 'not_found'}), 404\n    if job.is_finished:\n        return jsonify({'status': 'finished', 'result': job.result})\n    elif job.is_failed:\n        return jsonify({'status': 'failed', 'error': str(job.exc_info)})\n    else:\n        return jsonify({'status': 'queued'})\n\n@app.route('/pii_audit/<audit_id>', methods=['GET'])\ndef pii_audit(audit_id):\n    \"\"\"Retrieve encrypted PII for audit.\"\"\"\n    token = redis_conn.get(f\"pii:{audit_id}\")\n    if not token:\n        return jsonify({'error': 'Not found'}), 404\n    pii = decrypt_pii(token)\n    return jsonify({'pii': pii})\n\n# --- Main ---\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app.run(debug=True)",
                        "\"\"\"\nB2B SaaS MVP: Automated Dispute Evidence Collection & Submission\n\nFeatures:\n- Collects dispute evidence from Shopify orders.\n- Generates indexed, watermarked, and redacted PDFs using Puppeteer (via pyppeteer).\n- Interfaces with Stripe and PayPal APIs to submit evidence.\n- Uses job queues for background processing (via RQ and Redis).\n- Securely handles PII.\n- Flask-based API for MVP demonstration.\n\nRequirements:\n- pip install flask stripe paypalrestsdk pyppeteer shopifyapi redis rq python-dotenv reportlab\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport tempfile\nimport uuid\nimport json\nfrom flask import Flask, request, jsonify, send_file\nfrom rq import Queue\nfrom redis import Redis\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\nimport stripe\nimport paypalrestsdk\nimport shopify\nfrom pyppeteer import launch\nfrom reportlab.pdfgen import canvas\nfrom reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter\n\n# Load environment variables\nload_dotenv()\n\n# Flask app setup\napp = Flask(__name__)\n\n# Redis connection and RQ queue\nredis_conn = Redis(host='localhost', port=6379)\nqueue = Queue('jobs', connection=redis_conn)\n\n# Stripe setup\nstripe.api_key = os.getenv(\"STRIPE_API_KEY\")\n\n# PayPal setup\npaypalrestsdk.configure({\n    \"mode\": \"live\",  # or \"sandbox\"\n    \"client_id\": os.getenv(\"PAYPAL_CLIENT_ID\"),\n    \"client_secret\": os.getenv(\"PAYPAL_CLIENT_SECRET\")\n})\n\n# Shopify setup\nSHOPIFY_API_KEY = os.getenv(\"SHOPIFY_API_KEY\")\nSHOPIFY_PASSWORD = os.getenv(\"SHOPIFY_PASSWORD\")\nSHOPIFY_SHOP_NAME = os.getenv(\"SHOPIFY_SHOP_NAME\")\n\nshop_url = f\"https://{SHOPIFY_API_KEY}:{SHOPIFY_PASSWORD}@{SHOPIFY_SHOP_NAME}.myshopify.com/admin\"\nshopify.ShopifyResource.set_site(shop_url)\n\n# Secure PII Redaction\ndef redact_pii(data):\n    \"\"\"\n    Redacts PII from dictionary. For demo, redacts email, phone, address.\n    \"\"\"\n    redacted = dict(data)\n    for key in redacted:\n        if key in ['email', 'phone', 'address', 'name']:\n            redacted[key] = '[REDACTED]'\n    return redacted\n\n# PDF Generation with watermark and indexing\ndef generate_pdf(evidence_data, watermark_text=\"CONFIDENTIAL\"):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generates a watermarked, indexed PDF from evidence data.\n    \"\"\"\n    fd, pdf_path = tempfile.mkstemp(suffix=\".pdf\")\n    os.close(fd)\n    c = canvas.Canvas(pdf_path, pagesize=letter)\n    width, height = letter\n\n    # Index page\n    c.setFont(\"Helvetica-Bold\", 16)\n    c.drawString(72, height - 72, \"Evidence Index\")\n    c.setFont(\"Helvetica\", 12)\n    y = height - 100\n    for i, key in enumerate(evidence_data.keys()):\n        c.drawString(72, y, f\"{i+1}. {key}\")\n        y -= 20\n    c.showPage()\n\n    # Evidence pages\n    for key, value in evidence_data.items():\n        c.setFont(\"Helvetica-Bold\", 14)\n        c.drawString(72, height - 72, key)\n        c.setFont(\"Helvetica\", 12)\n        c.drawString(72, height - 100, str(value))\n        # Watermark\n        c.saveState()\n        c.setFont(\"Helvetica\", 40)\n        c.setFillGray(0.5, 0.5)\n        c.translate(width/2, height/2)\n        c.rotate(45)\n        c.drawCentredString(0, 0, watermark_text)\n        c.restoreState()\n        c.showPage()\n    c.save()\n    return pdf_path\n\n# HTML to PDF using pyppeteer for rich evidence\nasync def html_to_pdf(html_content, output_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Uses pyppeteer to render HTML to PDF.\n    \"\"\"\n    browser = await launch(headless=True)\n    page = await browser.newPage()\n    await page.setContent(html_content)\n    await page.pdf({'path': output_path, 'format': 'A4'})\n    await browser.close()\n\n# Stripe Evidence Submission\ndef submit_stripe_evidence(dispute_id, evidence_pdf_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Submits evidence PDF to Stripe dispute.\n    \"\"\"\n    with open(evidence_pdf_path, 'rb') as f:\n        file_upload = stripe.File.create(\n            purpose='dispute_evidence',\n            file=f,\n        )\n    stripe.Dispute.modify(\n        dispute_id,\n        evidence={'customer_communication': file_upload.id}\n    )\n    return file_upload.id\n\n# PayPal Evidence Submission\ndef submit_paypal_evidence(dispute_id, evidence_pdf_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Submits evidence PDF to PayPal dispute.\n    \"\"\"\n    # PayPal REST API does not support direct file upload for disputes,\n    # but you can add evidence as text or upload via their web portal.\n    # For demo, we attach as a note.\n    dispute = paypalrestsdk.Dispute.find(dispute_id)\n    with open(evidence_pdf_path, 'rb') as f:\n        note = {\n            \"note\": \"See attached evidence PDF.\",\n            \"evidence_type\": \"OTHER\"\n        }\n        dispute.add_evidence(note)\n    return True\n\n# Shopify Order Evidence Collection\ndef collect_shopify_evidence(order_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    Collects evidence from Shopify order.\n    \"\"\"\n    order = shopify.Order.find(order_id)\n    evidence = {\n        \"Order ID\": order.id,\n        \"Customer\": redact_pii({\n            \"name\": order.customer.first_name + \" \" + order.customer.last_name,\n            \"email\": order.email,\n            \"address\": order.shipping_address.address1 if order.shipping_address else \"\",\n            \"phone\": order.phone\n        }),\n        \"Items\": [line_item.name for line_item in order.line_items],\n        \"Total\": order.total_price,\n        \"Created At\": order.created_at,\n        \"Financial Status\": order.financial_status,\n        \"Fulfillment Status\": order.fulfillment_status\n    }\n    return evidence\n\n# Job queue task\ndef process_dispute_job(platform, dispute_id, order_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    Main job to collect evidence, generate PDF, and submit to Stripe/PayPal.\n    \"\"\"\n    # 1. Collect evidence\n    evidence = collect_shopify_evidence(order_id)\n    \n    # 2. Generate PDF\n    pdf_path = generate_pdf(evidence)\n    \n    # (Optional) Generate HTML evidence and convert to PDF\n    html_content = f\"<h1>Order Evidence</h1><pre>{json.dumps(evidence, indent=2)}</pre>\"\n    html_pdf_path = tempfile.mktemp(suffix=\".pdf\")\n    import asyncio\n    asyncio.get_event_loop().run_until_complete(html_to_pdf(html_content, html_pdf_path))\n    \n    # 3. SQLAlchemy(app)\nbcrypt = Bcrypt(app)\nPII_KEY = Fernet.generate_key()\nfernet = Fernet(PII_KEY)\n\nclass User(db.Model):\n    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)\n    email = db.Column(db.String(120), unique=True, nullable=False)\n    password_hash = db.Column(db.String(128), nullable=False)\n\nclass DisputeJob(db.Model):\n    id = db.Column(db.Integer, primary_key=True)\n evidence_pdf = db.Column(db.LargeBinary)\n    created_at = db.Column(db.DateTime, server_default=db.func.now())\n\ndef encrypt_data(data: bytes) -> bytes:\n    return fernet.encrypt(data)\n\ndef decrypt_data(token: bytes) -> bytes:\n    return fernet.decrypt(token)\n\n# Dummy implementations for test\ndef watermark_and_redact_pdf(html_content: str, watermark_text: str, redacted_fields: list) watermark_and_redact_pdf(html_content, watermark_text, redacted_fields)\n        encrypted_pdf = encrypt_data(pdf_data)\n        job.evidence_pdf = encrypted_pdf\n        job.status = 'ready'\n        db.session.commit()\n    except Exception as e:\n        job.status = 'failed'\n        db.session.commit()\n        raise\n\n@app.route('/register', methods=['POST'])\ndef register():\n    data =                         "\"\"\"\nB2B SaaS MVP: Automated Dispute Evidence Collection & Submission\n\nFeatures:\n- Evidence collection from Shopify orders\n- PDF generation with watermarking/redaction html_file.name.replace('.html', '.pdf')\n        # Node.js Puppeteer script path (should be in same directory)\n        script_path = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'puppeteer_pdf.js')\n    finally:\n            try:\n                os.unlink(html_file.name)\n            except Exception:\n                pass\n            try:\n                os.unlink(pdf_path)\n            except || '[]');\n    await page.evaluate((fields) => {\n        fields.forEach(f => {\n            document.body.innerHTML = document.body.innerHTML.replace(new RegExp(f, 'gi'), '[REDACTED]');\n        });\n    }, redacted);\n\n    // Watermark\n    await page.evaluate((text) => {\n        const watermark = document.createElement('div');\n        watermark.innerText = text;\n
